Abocco
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
A Vailian shouts over the din of the Wild Mare to get your attention, turning a great many heads to study your exchange.
He takes a hearty swig of his tankard.
Abocco is a novice bounty hunter fixer, looking for someone to take on his bounty contracts. Problem is, there are no takers, no matter how much he slurs his speech.
Interactions

Andres Williams.

Acolyte Kinnuq
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
A robed acolyte working for Nemnok, the Acolyte is a faithful follower of the "god" below, leading his vast team of scribes and acolytes in perusing the scrolls and tomes brought by the Junvik people to the Barrows.

16 you can avoid having to fight him. Then you can punch him in the gut for being insufferable.

Aenalys
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
A young woman reclines on the cushions, a hookah hose held delicately in one hand. Eyes closed, she sings to herself. Her voice is soft and inviting.
She doesn't move when she hears you approach, but slowly opens her eyes with a lazy smile.
Aenalys is a professional actor who belonged to a troupe that toured the
Aedyr Empire
. Performing classic works of literature to cheering audience and enjoying good wages amounted to a decent life when things were going well. However, she desired a more dependable audience and so picked up the trade of a courtesan.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests
.
Lost Dues in Good Faith
This character has
other interactions
.
Bringing
Aloth
along results in an unique interaction during the quest.
For
100
you can hire her services, listen to poetry, and receive Aenalys' Boon (+1
Explosives
and
Metaphysics
, +2
Perception
)
She occasionally stands up and walks over to her cabinet, giving you a good opportunity to pickpocket the
key
from her.
Quests
Lost Dues in Good Faith
:
Oswald
favoured her, and he often visited to listen to old epics in Eld Aedyran.

Akema
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
A Roparu who held a good job at the Luminous Bathhouse, but was fired for unprofessional behavior - gasping when she overheard a conversation she was supposed to be deaf to. Now she desperately looks for new employment in the Queen's Berth district, to avoid going back to
The Gullet
.

This character has
other interactions
.
Akema gives you a brief summary of Queen's Berth, pointing you in the direction of
The Brass Citadel
, the
Luminous Bathhouse
in

, and
Kahanga Palace
.

Amreo
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
An old man stretches his arms over his head and yawns, making a show of displaying his moistened physique.
Grandpa Amreo makes little secret of the fact that he cruises the establishment looking for... Opportunities.
Interactions
This character has
other interactions
.
During the conversation, Amreo's "knees begin to drift apart." The Watcher has reactions to this, and can put him in his place.
A
dwarven
or
orlan
Watcher can say
"No! My eyes!"
Intimidate
4: "Go admit to the steward you're treating this establishment like a brothel."
Further interaction (clicking the NPC) yields flavour text:
The old man winces, his eyes downcast
.

Anahāru

Anahāru
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
Anaharu was the previous priest of
Ngati
at
Tikawara
, one who lost the fight with
Ranga Ruānu
, but swore to continue fighting against the VTC nonetheless. By sacrificing his essence to the adra pillar at
Poko Kohara
, he entered the realm of adra and used his power to block the flow of souls, unleashing terrible storms on the region in a bid to counter
Vailian scheming
. He believes that not only is he carrying out Ngati's will and protecting the village, but that he's also protecting the people of Tikawara.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests
.
The Storms of Poko Kohara
Quests
The Storms of Poko Kohara
: Anaharu is confronted at the end of the quest.

Anniq
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
An elderly dwarf folds her arms, her disapproving frown warping the tattoos that encircle her face.
Anniq is the tattooed chieftain of the Junvik village to the far north of Deadfire. Unlike Tatok, she is a fervent believer in
Nemnok
and treats him like an actual god.

This character has
other interactions
.

Tatok
in dialogue upon first entering the area.

Apāro
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
A round-bellied man stands at ease before a cluster of hardened fighters, their fists balled and brows furrowed.
He is a particularly diplomatic Mataru of the Wahaki, which makes him stand out from among his peers. He is fully aware that the Huana are endangered by foreign powers, but is willing to give people a chance to prove themselves.

Arkemyr
is one of the infamous archmages of
Eora
, and appears in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
Arkemyr is an archmage of worldwide renown. The spells bearing his name focus largely on illusion and pain - qualities that he prizes in his personal life and teaching philosophy. Over the years he has fostered dozens of students, but none have graduated from their apprenticeship to Arkemyr's satisfaction - opting instead to leave his service in bitterness and resentment over the archmage's notoriously unfair treatment.
Fessina
, his latest apprentice, bears a particular disdain against Arkemyr, calling him the "Bringer of Foul Wind, the Teat of Suckling Imps, and the Herald of Dirty Slippers." He currently lives in Neketaka at Periki's Overlook, where he operates a local magic shop -
The Dark Cupboard
.
Arkemyr is a member of the
Circle of Archmagi
. Depending on who you ask, it's either Eora's equivalent of the Avengers or a club for bumbling fools jumped up on magic. As
Aloth
points out, their involvement is typically the worst possible outcome - as per the
Blackwash Falls
incident, in which the the Circle successfully vanished all water from an area to predictably catastrophic results. 
While Arkemyr is quite in favor of the former interpretation, that doesn't make him any less annoyed by having drawn the short straw and being settled with the duty of watching over the
Deadfire Achipelago
for the current decade, having to to relocate halfway across the known world to
his estate
.
He is disliked by other archmagi, especially
Llengrath
. He is a deceptive snake, after all: He relocated his estate to Neketaka after convincing the powers that be that the Kahanga Palace was structurally unstable... And financing the renovations.
Interactions
This character
starts
quests
.
Bekarna's Folly
This character is
involved in
quests
.
A Cordial Invitation
This character has
other interactions
.
With the
Waterlogged Journal
in your inventory, you can ask him about "The Sanguine Harvest".
If you wear
Arkemyr's Old Robe
, or if one of your companion wears them, this triggers unique dialogue with Arkrmyr.
If you killed
Concelhaut
in
The White March - Part I
or
Llengrath
in
The Forgotten Sanctum
, he brings this up.
With
Aloth
in the party, he will bring up the Blackwash Falls incident when Arkemyr asks for your help in preparing for the "worst possible outcome".
You can tattletale on
Fassina
for giving you the
key
to Arkemyr's Manor.
With Fassina in the party, he'll have a particularly unsavoury reaction towards her presence in the manor.
Quests
A Cordial Invitation
to
Bekarna's Folly
: Arkemyr invites you over to discuss his vault. Which you absolutely did not burgle. Ooops. As absolution, you are to raid the observatory of a fellow mage,
Bekarna
.
Companion reactivity
If you or a companion are wearing
Arkemyr's Old Robe
:
"Your robes - how alike they are to one I keep in my chambers." His eyes narrow to pinpricks.
"Your companion's robes - so similar to my own. How fascinating." His eyes narrow to pinpricks.
After one of the reactions below, he responds
"Again, fascinating." He swivels his gaze back to you.

Atello Valera's face is lined and weary, but his coat is tidily buttoned, his posture faultless.

Background
Her speech gets cut short as one of the vines about her midsection tightens its hold, nearly forcing the breath from her lungs.
Gritting her teeth, she braces against the vines and fights to steal back some breathing room.
Baltia is the sole surviving member of an ill-fated expedition to Motare. After her own expedition was wiped out, she was attacked and trapped by particularly aggressive vines that took and constricted her.

Bearn
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
Unlike the other survivors you've seen, this young man, despite a haggard look and a set of dirt-smeared, tattered clothes, wears a calm face and speaks with a steady voice.
Bearn is Elafa's son and unfortunately for Edér, not his son, as he knew his father before the Purges killed him. He lost his mother too, though on the cusp on adulthood, when the flu took her on Hasongo. Problem is, when he was lost in his grief, the
Partisans of the Lighted Path
exploited his vulnerability and molded him into a religious fanatic, bent on sacrificing his soul to the walking titan.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests
.

: He is who Edér wants to protect and hopefully not fail in the process.
He can be found outside the Storage Tower in Hasongo, to the left of Zuhira.
Trivia
He is voiced by
Sam Riegel
, who voices a number of other characters in the game.

Quests
Wasting Minds
Technical
GUID
22cc7192-b3be-4130-8950-57c7c5ad184b
Bekarna
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
One of the more interesting wizards in Eora, Bekarna's research into stars and celestial affairs was a subject of grave importance to the Deadfire, though not to the
Archmages
. When she presented her work to
the Circle of Archmagi
, she was laughed out into the streets. Undaunted, she continued her work, eventually crossing paths with the
Hand Occult
and becoming imprisoned in
The Halls Obscured
for seeking unauthorized revelation. As subject K-1121, her mental state steadily deteriorated, due to the isolation from her orrery that always helped her center herself.
Interactions
This character
starts
quests
.
Wasting Minds
This character has
other interactions
.
You can give her a sapphire on first encounter, receiving an adra ban in return.
Quests
Wasting Minds
: Meeting her starts the quest, focusing on restoring the memories and minds of the people imprisoned in the Collections.
Notes
Her
Avowed
encyclopedia entry states: "Bekarna is a recent addition to the Circle of Archmagi. She keeps a private library and observatory in the Deadfire Archipelago, where she researches the stars, the void, and the (highly theoretical) spiritual properties of meteors."

Biha
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
A woman thrashes a row of tunics and sarongs hanging from the rafters. Her pointed teeth are gritted in frustration, her lips set in a snarl.
The clothes are spotless, yet she swings a handful of reeds again and again, grunting with each blow.
Several children huddle together, whispering and looking on with red, tearful eyes.
Biha is one of the Roparu forced to live in
The Gullet
, ruthlessly exploited by other castes. Her only dream is to get off the island and emigrate to Rauatai, seeking a better future somewhere where the caste system doesn't condemn her to slow starvation.
She is
Botaro
's partner, and witnesses him being lowered into the Old City, essentially a form of execution for those who can't defend themselves from the monsters that lurk below.
Interactions
This character
starts
quests
.
All Aboard
Quests
All Aboard
: She wishes to obtain passage on a ship bound for
Rauatai
as means of escape from the conditions and the persecution she faces in
The Gullet
.

Botaro
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
You see a man being dragged along a rickety boardwalk toward a rusty cage that swings over the abyss. He strains against the guard's grip.
The guard delivers a savage backhand.
Botaro was accused of consorting with foreign criminals - and to keep the Roparu in line, "justice" was administered swiftly by the
Overseer
in the form of his immediate removal to the Old City far, far below.
Botaro is
Biha
's partner, and his death leaves her widowed and left to care for her three children alone.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests
.
All Aboard
This character has
other interactions
.
After starting
All Aboard
, his body can be found in the
Old City Overlook
a short distance west of the lift. You can interact with his soul to reveal some information about his last moments alive.
Quests
All Aboard
: Botaro can be seen being lowered into the Old City upon approaching the lift in
The Gullet
. Needless to say, he doesn't last long enough for you to get the opportunity to talk to him - alive at least.

Calandra
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
The head of the Pegleg Performers, a troupe of performers with a lengthy history in Dunnage (previously known as the Seabird Serenaders and the Jaxe-Finingen First Ensemble of Dunnage). The change in naming doesn't seem to have improved their fortunes, as they are bleeding actors, money, and audience fast. Calandra wants to improve the show: Get a better Eothas, better stage effects, and more!

.
Background

Impostor's Lament
, Angfor and his crew were forced to land on

after their ship sank. Without relief or a supply of food, they were forced to subsist on a diet of each other, slowly forming a terrifying cannibal cult.

======================================================================
PAGE: Carlo Fortuni
CATEGORIES: Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire characters
URL: https://pillarsofeternity.fandom.com/wiki/Carlo_Fortuni
======================================================================

Carlo Fortuni
Biography and appearance
Game
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
Race
Savannah
human
Gender
Male
Culture
Vailian Republics
Gameplay
Location
Dunnage
,
Lifter's Refuge
Carlo Fortuni
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
A trim man in practical, well-crafted leathers watches you from the corner of his eyes. When he catches you looking his way, his hand drifts casually to the dagger at his hip and lingers for a moment.
Then he smiles, the corners of his hazel eyes crinkling with genuine warmth, and waves you over.
Carlo was born to a family of merchants on the Pearl Coast, growing up learning his father's trade and geography. His good fortune continued, until he made the mistake of joining up with a company from Girrara that traded in beautiful weavings. Trouble is, the goods were produced by a kidnapped weaver named Bonisetta. When the
Watcher
's companion uncovered that crime, Carlo was caught up in the fallout and exiled from the Republics.
He fled to the Deadfire, seeking anonymity and whatever opportunities he can find.
Interactions
This character has
other interactions
.
Carlo offers training for
3,000
, offering +1 to Sleight of Hand and Diplomacy.

Cathŵenna
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
The kith present an odd trio, a broad-shouldered elf flanked by a tall aumaua and a wild-haired orlan. Each holds weapons at the ready as the woman steps forward. She bears an improvised flail made from a ball and chain.
Cathŵenna was imprisoned for ten years and broke her own ankle to release herself from chains, then joined up with
Hudango
and
Cemoc
as she fled into the Crookspur wilderness, becoming a persistent plague on the slavers there.

CHA_15_TK_Coralmason
GUID
020e3df2-c4be-469e-8aca-c6a44354e234
Coralmason
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
When you first enter the workshop, you find the Vailian scientist, Iverra, and a large aumaua man in heated conversation. He gestures wildly, his mouth is set in a hard grimace that bares his pointed teeth. Iverra regards him with her hands planted firmly on her hips.
When he spots, you his eyes widen.
Coralmason is, well, a coral mason on Sayuka. He's part of a team of scientists trying to find a way to stop the out-of-control coral growths around Sayuka. He's surmised that a magical disturbance is the source of the problem, located somewhere in the deep sea southeast of the island, once the location of an old Engwithan ruin
Cignath Mór
.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests
.
Overgrowth
Quests
Overgrowth
: He and
Iverra
think they've found the source of the coral growths on Sayuka, and naturally task you to investigate. He is found in the
workshop
, but will leave when you finish dialogue with him.

Degnos
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
A Vailian sailor down on his luck, Degnos needs to find his satchel in the luminous bathhouse, but without his captain present, the guards consider him little more than a thief. He loiters outside, trying to find someone who can help him. Of course, once you talk to the proprietor, he will reveal that Degnos tried to sneak into one of the rooms, telling a sob story in a lame attempt to avoid a ban.
Interactions
This character
starts
quests
.
Sealed Fate
This character has
other interactions
.

Avetta
, he will flee to the
Old City Overlook
. His corpse can be found near the lower center portion of the map.
Quests
Sealed Fate
: He asks you to retrieve his satchel.

He didn't last too long...

Internal Name
NPC_SD_Dereo
GUID
5ea127bc-e6c9-4b9e-a053-d1d970fd7df7
Dereo the Lean
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
A thin, long-limbed man holds a handkerchief in one hand and a threaded needle in the other. As you approach, he sets his handiwork aside, and you see an elaborate goldwork pattern embroidered around the edge - the same pattern that adorns his brilliant tunic.
You also notice a strange bulk beneath the thin fabric of his trouser legs that runs from hip from ankle. He leans forward with a squeak of leather and a rattle of metal. You see something protruding above his boots - the bottom of a leg brace.
Dereo is an old style Príncipi, back from a time when that meant loyalty and unity. Although he's not fond of the new blood flooding the organization, he recognizes the fact that they are necessary if the Princes are to stand against Rauatai, VTC, and the Huana.
Interactions
This character
starts
quests
.
The Cornett's Call
This character is
involved in
quests
.
Delver's Row
Food for Thought
Quests
The Cornett's Call
: He sends you to retrieve ancient Huana artifacts with a bigger game afoot.
Delver's Row
/
Food for Thought
: Dereo can give you passage to the row during
The Cornett's Call
.
Trivia
Dereo the Lean is possibly inspired by
Gustavo Fring
from the TV series
Breaking Bad
.

Drowsy Puke
is a character in
The Forgotten Sanctum
.
Background
The imp is furiously mixing powders and herbs into a mortar and pestle. It leers at you, showing off a row of pointed teeth and a long, flicking tongue.
Drowsy Puke is an amateur chemist responsible for providing drugs to Arkemyr. The dosage he uses is enough to knock out an ogre and feeds the archmage's addiction mightily, but the imp doesn't mind, taking a perverse personal satisfaction out of the job. Drowsy has a penchant for a bit of anarchy, and a secret plan to overthrow Arkemyr and free the imps from his oppression.
Interactions
This character is a
merchant
.
Sells: An equivalent of "rooms"
This character has
other interactions
.
You can find two additional recipes to add new resting options.
With
Alchemy
10 or the Scientist background, you can tell he's not a trained apothecary. With a further 1 Alchemy, you can tell that the dosage is enough to bring down an ogre.
You can hand him some
Ripple Sponge
to help him with his concoction.
If you're wearing
Arkemyr's Old Robe
, you can give it to Drowsy Puke to help him overthrow
Arkemyr
with the other imps in his manor (see below).
You can introduce Drowsy Puke to
Nemnok
if you have him equipped as a pet. They'll discuss their "plans", and if you've already given him the robe you'll get some unique dialogue.
If you have
Concelhaut's Skull
, Nemnok says:
"TELL SKULL TO STOP BITING NEMNOK IN SLEEP." Nemnok aims a venomous look down your pack at Concelhaut's leering skull.
Rooms
While not an inn in the traditional respect, you can pay Drowsy Puke to mix you up a potion which will knock you out cold for a few hours.
Light Snooze
(
100
): +10% Max Health
Deep Slumber
(
250
): +10
, 5% resistance against Spells
Entrancing Daze
(
500
):
Resistance
to
Intellect afflictions
(after giving him
Recipe - Entrancing Daze
)
Invigorating Nightmares
(
500
):
Resistance
to
Resolve afflictions
(after giving him
Recipe - Invigorating Nightmares
)
Reactivity
Drug trip
While sampling the drugs, Drowsy Puke's dialogue and changes to that of a sophisticated scientist. You can choose to ride the trip out, which will result in some rather deep, humorous, and ominous dialogue.
Dialogue
Condition
Time passes. You wonder if Eothas could build a castle so large that even he couldn't tip it over.
You wonder if he'd consider rebuilding yours.
You wonder if all the boys in Lipasalis are as handsome as Rekke.
If
Rekke
is recruited, and he has learned
Aedyran
and told you of Lipasalis.
You wonder if Concelhaut ate the last of your candied nuts.
If you have both
Concelhaut's Skull
and
Candied Nuts
in your inventory.
Companion
Dialogue
Edér
"What if all pets are just one pet, but we see them through a variety of lenses? Like dancing shadows cast by a campfire against a barn wall."
Aloth
(as
Iselmyr
)
"I should've killt the eld bastard. Should've teired his arm clear off. If the laddie hadn't stopped me..."
Maia Rua
"You all right there, captain? Looking a little parched. Let me get you some water."
She then gives you a
Water
.
While Maia rifles through her belongings, Ishiza stares at you. His eyes are mirrors, but you don't see yourself in them. You see only birds. An endless sky, filled with birds. You are nowhere to be found in the avian oblivion.
Pallegina
"Di verus, you will sweat yourself dry. What did you do to the Watcher, imp?"
Serafen
What none've told you, is that Ngati's but a child, the daughter of the depths, whose own parents are so vast, so impossible, that they could swallow every island in the Deadfire and hunger for more. They slumber in the darkness below the waves, wrapped in their own fleshy cocoons, watching through their daughter's eyes. Waiting.
Xoti
"Well dang, Watcher. Save some of that for me!"
Rekke
(Only if the Watcher is NOT a
death godlike
, and
Rekke
has learned Aedyran)
"It was supposed to be a joke - a sparkbomb, just to scare him. He shouldn't have caught fire. I'm sorry, I'm so sorry... please, mother/father, don't make me leave. I'll die out there."
His sobs are muffled, distorted - as if they come to you down a long hall.
Tekēhu
As though sensing your rising anxiety, Tekēhu gently takes you by the shoulder and pulls you into a warm embrace. His skin is soft, and he makes a shushing sound like waves battering the shore. You feel safe.
Imp uprising
With
Arkemyr's Old Robe
equipped, the imp asks that you give it to him as part of some cunning plan.
When asked for details, he refuses to tell you anything more. However, if you managed to rob
Arkemyr's Manor
as part of
The Archmage's Vault
without drawing suspicion to yourself (i.e. talking down all the imps and not entering combat), he says that he trusts your sneaking skills, and tells you that he plans to dress up as Arkemyr and stage an uprising in order to take over the manor with
Nemnok the Devourer
and the rest of the imps.
If you choose to give him the robe, he gives you a
Coral Snuff
,
Deadeye
,
Ripple Sponge
,
Svef
,
Whiteleaf
, and a
Forgetful Night
as thanks.
It is unknown whether anything actually comes of Drowsy Puke's plan.

Ehrys
is a character in
Beast of Winter
.
Background
A ninety-year old Glamfellen, Ehrys is the estranged sister of
Harbinger Brythe
. She is a talented, intense personality with a zealous belief in a particularly extreme interpretation of the cult of Rymrgand. She has joined up with these extremists on an expedition to
the Dead Floe
, to claim it for the Beast. She considers the Harbingers to be too soft to properly worship Rymrgand. In fact, she despises anything to do with the mortal kith of Eora, desiring nothing more than becoming a rime construct and standing eternal vigil over the temple to the god of decay.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests

The Last Pilgrimage

: She desires to become a construct. Her sister wants her back. There can be only one (choice).

is a character and recruitable
crew member
in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
Eld Engrim appears to be in sound condition, though his waxed jacket is soaked through. He appraises you with bleary-eyed amusement.
A deck hand reeking of rum, Eld Engrim is a veteran of the seas, together with all the usual accouterments: A smile lacking teeth, balding head, waxed jacket... Of note is the fact that he's apparently an acquaintance of
Durance
.
Interactions
This character is a potential
crew member
of
The Defiant
.
Novice Cannoneer
Novice Surgeon
Personality: Drunkard, Religious
This character is
involved in
quests
.
Helping Hands
This character has
other interactions
.
A priest of
Magran
has some unique dialogue with Eld Engrim.
Eld Engrim will have a reaction regarding the outcome of
Durance
's questline in
Pillars of Eternity
.
He has some dialogue with
Vela
, and she has taken to calling him "Uncle Engrim".
Quests
Helping Hands
: Eld Engrim can be retrieved in the course of the quest.
Dialogue
Introductory dialogue
Eld Engrim:
"Aye. Magran learns us poor bastards that a little excitement's good for the heart."
As a
priest
of
Magran
Watcher:
"The flames reveal all in time, brother."
If
Durance
was recruited, but was killed or you didn't convince him of Magran and Woedica's plot:
Watcher:
"The last Magranite to travel with me wasn't quite up to the goddess' challenge."
Engrim:
"Aye. Poor Durance. May the mad whoreson see better days come the next turn of the Wheel."
If
Durance
was recruited, wasn't killed, and you convinced him of Magran and Woedica's plot:
Watcher:
"The last Magranite to travel with me almost went mad because of his goddess' trials."
Engrim:
"Aye, but almost mad ain't fully mad. Ah, Old Durance. The goddess shan't forge another like him in our lives, captain."
If
Vela
is present
Vela:
"Can we go back on the ship now?"
Vela rocks back on the heels of her feet, watching you both.
Watcher:
"Vela, don't let Engrim be a bad influence while I'm gone."
Eld Engrim:
"That's unkind. Yer the one decided to pluck this wean from the wilds of
Eir Glanfath
. Blame that stone steward of yers for bringing the furry maid along."
If the Watcher is an
orlan
Eld Engrim:
"Eh... no slight to yer kind, of course, captain."
He chuckles and nods in your direction.
Vela:
"Uncle Engrim, you promised me ale."
Eld Engrim:
"Later, sweetie. Uncle Engrim's thirsty, too."
He absentmindedly taps on his chest, near his heart, sounding the thunk of something metal beneath the priest's jacket.
Banter with
Irrena
upon approaching the campfire:
Eld Engrim:
"I'll boil up some water. We'll have a spy at that leg of yers."
Irrena:
"Should have seen me with that barrel, Engrim. I showed it who's boss."
Eld Engrim:
"Mm. Magran gives some of us simpler trials than others."
Banter with
Beodul
upon approaching the campfire:
Eld Engrim:
"Should have known you'd come out of this in one piece, you old crank."
Beodul:
"I'd rather die than let ye savor the ship's last drop of ale."
Banter with
Vela
upon approaching the campfire:
Eld Engrim:
"May be time to wrangle a boar, afore the weakness of hunger sets in."
Vela:
"Boars are mean!"
Eld Engrim:
"Aye, maid, but I'm hungrier than they are mean."

Elias Zelen
Biography and appearance
Game
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
Race
Wood
elf
Gender
Male
Gameplay
Location
The King's Coffin
,
Dunnage
Elias Zelen
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
You find a lanky blond elf flipping through a book of Aedyran poetry by the artist Scilba. His armor is well-worn and well-kept, and bears on its breast the image of a double-headed eagle holding a sword and crown.
Looking more closely, you notice that with his free hand he's picking a padlock.
Elias is an aristocratic elf with plenty of secrets, though few he deigns to share. One story he does share is his expedition in backwoods
Readceras
, and a hoard of books he discovered that belonged to a Readceran priest. He then settled in Dyrwood, tutoring the children of a noble family and falling for the governess. Years passed until he suddenly became consumed by a special kind of wanderlust that forced him to leave his wife in her bed and walk out the door with barely the clothes on his back. He hopes that Deadfire will be the adventure he longed for.
Interactions
This character has
other interactions
.
For
3,000
he trains you for +1 Explosives and Mechanics.
Behind the scenes
He is voiced by
Peter Kenny
, who is more popularly known as the narrator of
The Witcher
series of audiobooks. Kenny also voices
Captain Furrante
and
Shrimp
.

Enoi
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
An elderly Roparu man squints in your direction before blinking profusely. He hobbles closer, bare feet slapping the splintered floorboards of his abode.
Enoi is the informal leader of the Roparu in the Gullet, a man as thin and ravaged by malnutrition that he seems more like a walking corpse. Yet he lives - seeing and hearing much more than the Mataru think he does.

Ernezzo
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
He peers at you through half-moon spectacles. His face is hidden behind a thick but well-groomed beard, and his eyes constantly dart between you and the doorway.
Ernezzo is a Vailian with a talent for 'acquisition' and 'distribution' - a smuggler and a black market specialist, in other words. He has plenty of connections across the world, including a svef supply line reaching as far as Defiance Bay.
Interactions
This character is a
merchant
.
Sells: Weapons, armor, ingredients. Also sells the unique items
Garari Cuirass
and
The Red Hand
. Completing
The Cornett's Call
will grant you a 10% discount in his store.
This character is
involved in
quests
.
Harsh Medicine
Trade Secrets
This character has
other interactions
.
Killing Ernezzo (or having him killed during
Harsh Medicine
) will give you a 10% discount at
Spindle Man's Store
.
Quests
Harsh Medicine
: He can provide the medicine - for a price.

“
Lady Ezzali Bardatto. Custom dictates I say 'at your service,' but I have not the time for such lies.
”
Ezzali Bardatto
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
. She can be found in her study in
Bardatto Estate
.
Background
The head of the Bardatto family and owner of the largest bank backing the
Vailian Trading Company
's financial endeavors. Ezzali is curt, direct, and has little patience for fools or people who enjoy wasting her time. After all, it's her bank that shoulders the burden of Deadfire operations.
Ezzali is the mother of
Nera Bardatto
and
Larro Bardatto
.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests
.
A Sinking Feeling
Family Pride
This character has
other interactions
.
With
Insight
/
Religion
1 you can notice
Hylea
's stamp on her desk.
Quests
A Sinking Feeling
: She wants you to investigate the rumors regarding a
Valera
-driven plot against her family.
Family Pride
: You can either mediate peace between the feuding families, or side with either one and drive tensions higher.
Trivia
Despite claiming to be a
Goldpact Knights
paladin, she is actually a
Kind Wayfarers
paladin, with the Wayfarer-specific variant of
Flames of Devotion
/
Eternal Devotion
.

Fetid Spray
Upload image
Biography and appearance
Game

Fetid Spray
is a character in
The Forgotten Sanctum
.
Background
The imp turns to you and lets out a quick puff of vile spray from an orifice that abruptly snaps shut.
Fetid Spray is the other of the pair of imps sent by Arkemyr to support the excavations of the Black Isles and acts as both messenger and vendor.
Interactions
This character is a
merchant
.
Sells: Consumables and rare ingredients.
This character has
other interactions
.
Gives you some
Simple Instructions
from
Arkemyr
.
Gives
Fessina
An Assignment for Fassina
, also from Arkemyr.
Grants
Essence of Imp Spray
after returning
The Alchemy of Imp Spray
to
it
If you're wearing
Arkemyr's Old Robe
, Fetid Spray has quite a few lines of unique dialogue as he mistakes you for
Arkemyr
.

First Mate Fallon
Biography and appearance
Game

Race
Meadow
human
Gender
Female
Gameplay
Location
Radiant Court
First Mate Fallon
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
Fallon recites a series of poems when you first enter
Radiant Court
.
Interactions
This character has no special interactions.
Trivia
First Mate Fallon is likely a reference to beat poetess
Philippa Fallon
's scene in the 1958 movie,
High School Confidential!
, where a similar structured poem is recited.
"My old captain was a drinker from the day he was born to the day he died."
-
My old man was a bread stasher all his life.

Frightened Child
Biography and appearance
Game
The Forgotten Sanctum
Race
Human
Gender
Female
Gameplay
Location
Hall of Reconfiguration
Drops
Scourge of Bezzello
Frightened Child
is a character in
The Forgotten Sanctum
. She is one of the subjects being observed in the
Hall of Reconfiguration
.
Background
As the Chief Librarian instructed, we have redacted the child's home village from every available map. The work is taxing on our more covert agents, but it is a public servce we cannot let slip. Some graves should be forgotten.
When we arrived it was a ghost town in the truest sense of the word. Men and women conjured from memory and imagination walked the streets, going about their daily duties, ignorant of their own spectral nature. Stepping through their own rotted coprses.
All was silent save the music.
We followed it to the town square, where we found the child playing, the blood of her kin spattered across her instrument. She said – sang, really – that she could not control herself, begged us to help her stop.
We promised.
It was in poor taste to betray her trust, but at least her talents will be confined to the Collections. Confined and, in time, harnessed.
All she wanted was help to control her powers.
Interactions
This character has
other interactions
.
Found in the Bloody Champer, (north east) in the
Hall of Reconfiguration
. When you enter the enclosure, she will utter one word, "M-mother?", before summoning her spectral friends and attacking you.
The
Note on the Child
gives some backstory about the Child.
Xoti will give a short prayer, or words of kindness, upon her death: "Gaun take you and keep you, child."
Behind the scenes
Systems designer
Andy Artz
is credited for the design of the fight with the Frightened Child. In a stream, he said that the fight was of his favourite things that he designed in
Deadfire
.

PAGE: Fyonlecg

======================================================================

Fyonlecg
Upload image
Biography and appearance

The Forgotten Sanctum
Race
Elf

and
Hand Occult
Statistics
Class
Wizard

Oratory of Wael

Annotated History
Fyonlecg
is one of the archmages of
Eora
, appearing  in
The Forgotten Sanctum
.
Background
An Aedyran elf and former member of the
Hand Occult
and
The Circle of Archmagi
.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests
.
Annotated History
Quests
Annotated History
: The archmage is encountered in the course of the quest and promptly kills Maura.
Behind the scenes
“
For one, I wanted a more "traditional" villain for this DLC. We were doing a dungeon delve with a bunch of weird stuff in it, so there were certain beats I wanted to be straightforward or immediately understandable. So self-obsessed elf archmage partly arose from that - and where do we get our ideas of what's traditional and classic if not from Baldur's Gate, its influences, and the stuff those games have influenced since?
At the same time, I wanted someone who would reflect Aloth to an extent. An argument could be made (and Edér makes it, if you've got him and Aloth in the party in the Heart of Mystery, and the farmer dislikes the latter) that Fyonlecg is Aloth through a glass darkly. He's the worst possible version of Aloth.
Plus I knew that Aedyr Elf Wizard was a common enough player character type (it's mine, come to think of it!) that Fyonlecg could reflect the Watcher, too.
One of the subtler themes that runs through all three of the DLCs is an examination of how the Engwithan gods treat those who serve them. To what extent (if at all) can the Watcher trust the entities that, say, would shove a favored servant into a statue to run a personal fight club for two thousand years? What reward can the Watcher possibly expect from the likes of Berath for doing their will? But what's the alternative? What else could the Watcher do with the power they've amassed? At what point would they graduate from useful tool to threat to be crushed?
His half-faced state was meant largely to communicate that he'd gone through part of the process that created the other eyeless entities within the Halls Obscured. (I personally think it resonates thematically, too, on a bunch of different levels - reflecting on his particular ambitions towards recognition, the "wisdom" of the Circle in general, and the capriciousness of Wael -  but interpretation doesn't belong to the author.)
As for his performance, I cast Dale Rapley based solely on his audition, which blew me entirely away. He seemed to immediately understand the character's underpinnings and brought them to life, adding depth to a character that I would argue isn't wildly deep (in comparison to, say, Neriscyrlas).
”
~
OEI_Alex
Gallery
Fyonlecg Unmasked

Ganor
is a character in

.
Background
You are greeted by a tall, carefully composed man. The crescent moon in the center is his forehead glows faintly.
Up close, the careful tailoring of his opal-adorned robes and their immaculate cleanliness speak to a deep well of vanity.
Ganor is the proprietor and owner of the Luminous Bathhouse and a walking advertisement for the kind of pampering and opulence to be found within its halls.

Geirvard Calder
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
. He can be met on the balcony of the
Kahanga Palace
, in the
Serpent's Crown
district of
Neketaka
.
Background
You find a young man with long, blond hair drawn back in a simple club. His clothes are spare but well-tailored, and his armor, a fine brigantine in blue and silver, is polished to a shine.
He leans casually to one side, a clean hand on his hip, and sighs, bored. His eyes light up when he sees you.
Geirvard is the youngest scion of a noble house, who used the wealth and privilege afforded to him by birth to pursue a life of adventure across the Deadfire Archipelago. Although he's not much of a warrior, he's a capable storyteller, wizard, cartographer, and a veteran explorer.
Interactions
This character has
other interactions
.

, +1

) for
3,000
.
Behind the scenes
Geirvard Calder is one of the 10
backer created NPCs
, created as part of
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
's crowdfunding campaign.

PAGE: Giacolo
CATEGORIES: Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire characters
URL: https://pillarsofeternity.fandom.com/wiki/Giacolo
======================================================================

Giacolo
Biography and appearance
Game
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
Race
Ocean
human
Gender
Male
Gameplay
Location
Dunnage
,
Lifter's Refuge
Quests
The Man of Chimes
Giacolo
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
An animancer from the Vailian Republics, Giacolo has devoted his life to researching the
godlike
. Inspired by the work of Todh Beylecg, he has determined that godlikes all have an unique chime within their soul that defines who they are - and even developed a method of modifying or disrupting it.
He met the 12 year old
Pallegina
at the academy she was attending and when the distraught girl threatened suicide if he didn't at least try to remove the chime that was changing her into
Hylea
's kin. He performed the experiment. Although it cost him a lifetime ban from the academy, the severing of the chime allowed Pallegina to achieve a modicum of normalcy in her life, looking like her calabandra kin, rather than a twisted bird.
In recent years, he developed a method by which one may detect a godlike fetus in the mother's womb. This has led to his abduction by a crew of godlike, who consider his discovery a potential threat - and have held him hostage since.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests
.
The Man of Chimes
Quests
The Man of Chimes

Background
You find a middle-aged dwarf tied to a post, a pile of bloody refuse scattered at his feet. His beard is a matted mess, and his face is streaked with dirt. Despite his haggard state, he twists against his bonds when you approach.
Giordu is the last remaining sane member of the crew, a capable deckhand and a budding cook... Who specializes in cooking kith meat. Apparently he was the next thing on the menu.

Granis Yirgar
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
You meet a tall, brown-haired man dressed in full plate mail. That might not normally catch your eye, but his mail is unusual, colored a deep green and emblazoned with the image of a golden tree.
Hand on the pommel of his sword, he watches the crowd go by with keen eyes, relaxed yet fully alert. He narrows his eyes when he spots you.
Granis is the son of a disgraced noble family, who lost his father and brothers to the executioner's axe, while his mother and sister were thrown out to the street. He harbors the executioners no ill will, as it was a deserved fate. With nothing to their name but a trunk full of heirlooms, including the armor he wears, Granis donned the family name, trying to redeem himself as one of the Shieldbearers.
Interactions
This character has
other interactions
.
This character offers
training
(+1
Athletics
, +1
Survival
) for
3,000
.
A paladin class Watcher of the
The Shieldbearers of St. Elcga
has some unique dialogue with Granis.
Behind the scenes
Granis Yirgar is one of the 10
backer created NPCs
, created as part of
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
's crowdfunding campaign.

Gameplay
Location
Ukaizo Harbor
Quests
The City Lost to Time
“
You are the first kith to visit the shores of lost Ukaizo, and you will be the last.
We hope this puts your brilliant mind at ease.
”
Guardian of Ukaizo
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
The creature stares down at you with only dim recognition of your presence. Water drips down the tip of its mallet-like head.
In the days of old
Ukaizo
, there lived three dragons. As servants of
Ngati
, they swore to protect the islands and adra of the
Deadfire Archipelago
with the aid of the
Huana
who ruled there. This agreement served both the dragons and the Huana well for countless decades.
And then the
Engwithans
arrived.
The Engwithans were quick to endear themselves to their Huana hosts, and together these two great societies constructed machines across the archipelago with the power to sort, sequester, and destroy souls. Many thousands of Huana willingly sacrificed themselves to aid in the machines' creation, for they believed the Engwithans' project to be a noble one.
The Engwithan machine built at Ukaizo was the most precious of them all. Knowing they would need a guardian to protect it, the Engwithans entreated the three dragon servants of Ngati with an offer - the Engwithans would grant the dragons eternal life at the cost of their eternal service. The dragons thus allowed the Engwithans to tether their souls to a single beast, the Guardian of Ukaizo, and rejoiced in their new, undying form.
But the Guardian of Ukaizo's celebrations were to be short-lived. When the Engwithans sacrificed their society on the altar of apotheosis, the god who would become Ondra called down a great storm upon the city of Ukaizo and the surrounding islands, so intent was she to hide the evidence of the Engwithans' ascent to artificial godhood.
And so it was the Guardian of Ukaizo became the keeper of a dead city, bound in body to forever protect a place that no longer existed.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests
.
The City Lost to Time
Quests
The City Lost to Time
: The Guardian is the final enemy standing in the way to the lost city and its bounty of knowledge. You can pester him with questions to gain a lot of lore, if you Have Athletics 5 and Bluff 4, History 4, or a Cipher or Chanter class.
Behind the scenes
He was voiced by
Andrew Wincott
.

Gulfaryc
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
Born in 2767 AI, Gulfaryc is a veteran of the Steel Garrote, who decided to embark on one last quest to spend his twilight years not as a nameless elder, but as a hero of the Steel Garrote. On 2 Fonivèrno, 2827, the day of his sixtieth birthday, he departed the Empire to seek of a legendary mace blessed by
Woedica
herself, the Magistrate's Cudgel. Together with three other veterans,
Arnfryda
,
Carmet
, and
Blidh
he set out to the
Deadfire Archipelago
, traveling it up and down to find a single clue as to where the mace can be located. Finally, on 17 Majestu, they picked up its trail, leading to a long-forgotten
subterranean temple
to
Woedica
, where they found the
Magistrate's Cudgel
perched in the lap of the statue. The mighty soul of the mace compelled them to stay and protect it, lest it be carried away from its resting place. So they stayed, old men and women basking in the glory of the Exiled Queen, sustained by what little they could find on the island.
Interactions
This character has no special interactions.

Handsome Eliam
is a character and recruitable
crew member
in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
An enigmatic and loyal godlike from the Dyrwood, Eliam has been abducted by Crookspur slavers and broken for sale as a particularly exotic piece of... merchandise.
Interactions
This character is a potential
crew member
of
The Defiant
.
Novice Helmsman
Novice Cook
Personality: Enigmatic, Loyal
This character is
involved in
quests
.
A Shrewd Proposition
Clearing Out Crookspur
Cruel Cargo
This character has
other interactions
.
After buying him from the slavers (you can autobuy him for
2,000
, or if you bid sparingly for
1,200
), you can either have him join your crew as a slave or free him and then offer him a job on your ship or suggest that he head to the
Temple of Berath
in
Neketaka
.
By winning the auction, you are granted an audience with
Master Kua
to finalize the deal (the amount isn't deducted during the auction, but you still have to have the appropriate amount on hand). In meeting with Kua, you can offer your services instead of payment, making the exchange effectively free.
Quests
A Shrewd Proposition
,
Clearing Out Crookspur
,
Cruel Cargo
: He can be purchased to get an audience with
Master Kua
.
Trivia
If he joins your crew as a slave, his daily wage will be
0
. Additionally he'll be wearing a
Ragged Robe
while on the ship, instead of a
Vailian Frock Coat
, though these are the only differences.

Harbinger Brythe
is a character in
Beast of Winter
.
Background
A nearly sixty year old Glamfellen, Brythe came to the Dead Floe ten years ago and helped the Harbingers of Dusk in any way she could. She has no particular talent, being a jack-of-all-trades who can mend wounds, weave baskets, and brew some mighty fine booze. In fact, she was searching for her estranged sister,
Ehrys
, hoping to mend fences with her. Her sister was thirty years her senior and as far as Brythe was concerned, always the smarter, more confident one, who always knew better than other when it came to matters of religion.
Interactions
This character
starts
quests
.

,

Quests

more
fanatical zealots worshiping Rymrgand, who dwell on top of the glacier.
Completing her first quest will begin
The Last Pilgrimage
: Return to the temple to search for her sister, Ehrys.

Harbinger Leksi
is a character in
Beast of Winter
.
Background
This sculpture, carved from a block of ice, towers over a Glamfellen woman. She moves about the scultpure, a chisel in one hand, a mallet in the other. Her scrutiny clings to it as if it might melt it.
Leksi hails from the White that Wends and learned the art of sculpture from her mother, the same way she learned how to skin a seal or hone an obsidian blade. Ice is her favored material, due to its impermanence, and she's keenly available that few places can appreciate an ice carver such as her - even in the White that Wends, where art goes unappreciated if it doesn't serve a function or can't be carried on your person. Her current work is a representation of
the Beast of Winter
,
Rymrgand
's avatar.
Interactions
This character has
other interactions
.
Artists
have an unique interaction with her.

Harbinger Valbrendhür
is a character in
Beast of Winter
.
Background
The man stands from his fire and brushes his hands together, a smile splitting his patchy ice-colored beard.
Valbrendhür runs the Tip of the Iceberg, the common house located at
Harbingers' Watch
. He follows
Vatnir
out of the belief that the end of all things is inevitable, rejecting the notion advanced by Berathian priests that the Wheel turns endlessly. He arrived at this conclusion after discovering a camp full of frozen Glamfellen at the bottom of a ravine in the White that Wends.

High Priest Kasu
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
An ailing aumaua priest regards your approach with curiosity. He coughs into a sleeve stained with a spatter of silvery flecks.
Kasu is at the end of his cycle and has been purifying his soul for weeks now, to prepare to hand the temple over to his apprentice. He considers himself a flawed messenger and priest to Berath, as he's no death godlike, and for this reason he also purposefully tortures his body to hasten the death  - which will come in time, when he surrenders his heart from his chest. However, his ambition is to complete the gathered tomes of Berath before he dies, by adding the long-lost Eulogy to Yseyr from the Hanging Sepulchers to the temple's collection.
Interactions
This character
starts
quests
.
Eulogy for the Dead
Quests
Eulogy for the Dead
: And since you're the only one touched by Berath in a
long
time, you're the only chance for him to complete the collection, so to speak.
Trivia
Voiced by same voice actor who voiced
Maerwald
in
Pillars of Eternity
.

Ifren is a fortune telling machine, once-kith, who got on
Arkemyr
's bad side when he and an orlan partner attempted to break in to
Arkemyr's Manor
. He now lives in debt of Arkemyr at
The Dark Cupboard
, telling vague fortunes to customers.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests
.
The Archmage's Vault
This character has
other interactions
.
Can tell your fortune for
1
.
Quests
The Archmage's Vault
: For
500
(and an hour of your time), or with Intimidate 4/Bluff 4, Ifren will tell you about the tunnel leading from the
Luminous Bathhouse
to
Arkemyr's Manor
, as he once broke into the manor using those tunnels.
Other interactions
If you insult him after he tells you about the break-in, he'll throw coins at you, and you'll receive an injury (
Concussion
). You'll be unable to interact with Ifren after this.
Ifren will tell your fortune for one pire:
"I see a fork in the road. There's a statue of a... human. Someone in robes. Take the left fork. If you go right, it could get ugly. Don't ask me why."
"I see a... house. Four walls, a ceiling, a floor. All wood. If you sleep there four nights straight, your one true love will pass by in the street. Be quick before the bard in red steals her away."
"I see... an island. Its shores are pitted, wreathed in fire, but you are bound to go there. Someone awaits you. A man, I think. An old friend."
"I see a woman with... black hair. No, red hair. Very dark red. Or maybe it really is black. She'll want you to recover her... wedding ring. When she pays you, be careful - there's a scorpion hidden in her coin purse. I know not why."
"I see a... bucket. No, a ship! You're going to embark on a journey very soon... or have you already? If you encounter a man in... a hat, you must be careful not to speak to him. The consequences are too dire."
Behind the scenes
He was voiced by
Andrew Wincott
.

Imuani
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
This grizzled old aumaua woman looks like she's been left in the sun to dry. Her skin is so worn and weathered, it's hard to tell her wrinkles from her scars.
Imuani sells only the finest armor and weapons, tested on the denizens of The Gullet.

Irrena
is a character and recruitable
crew member
in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
A founding member of the Defiant's crew and one of the survivors of the Deadfire welcome. Although she survived, she didn't do so unscathed: She suffered a broken knee and a nasty gouge along the length of her shin. It's the result of her trying to fasten the mess on the deck when the ship hit ground. A barrel crunched her leg.
Interactions

crew member
of
The Defiant
.

Iverra
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
A plump, middle-aged woman stands beside the crates. Her clothing is rumpled and her hair matted, but her eyes twinkle with triumph.
One of the most renowned scientists in the Vailian Republics, Iverra's dream focused on making the depths of Eora's waters accessible to kith. To that end, she has pioneered a number of diving technologies, including her famous
diving helmet
and a number of spells, like Renove mes Aires - "Renewal of Air". However, the profit-minded attitude of the Republics and the resulting lack of funding for her research led to her contacting the
Royal Deadfire Company
and offering them their services. Fleet Master Okaya arranged to have her smuggled out of the Republics in a crate, which is where the Watcher comes in.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests
.
A Matter of Import
Quests
A Matter of Import
: She's the business. Well, partly at least.

Jacob Harker
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
At the bar, you find a tall man with salt gray hair and strikingly bright blue eyes. His face sports a handful of long scars that continue down his neck and disappear beneath the collar of his shirt.
He looks up from wiping down the counter when you approach and gives you a broad, disarming smile.
Jacob Harker is the innkeeper of
The King's Coffin
on
Dunnage
. In a previous life, he was the infamous Red King, bane of Vailian merchants on the  high seas, exacting his revenge for the Republics driving his father out of business. After a while, however, he tired of the pirate hunters, so he paid off his crew, beached the dhow at Dunnage, and started a tavern.
Interactions
This character is a
merchant
.
Sells: Food, drink, rooms and supplies.
This character is
involved in
quests
.
Iron Gut
A Tidy Performance
Rooms
Jacob rents rooms. The available options are:
The Bilge Pump (free)
Sailors' Berth (
200
): +10% Max Health, +1 enemies engaged
Officers' Quarters (
400
): +2
Might
and
Concentration
Captain's Cabin (
800
): +3
Perception
, +1 max empower points
Quests
Iron Gut
: Jacob Harker will sell a vial of
Fire Kelp Extract
, an ingredient for Ondra's Bile, required for the
Iron Gut
task.
A Tidy Performance
: He will sell you the freedom of
Taerna
, required for the
A Tidy Performance
task.
Behind the scenes
The character portrait for Jacob Harker is based on
Tim Cain
, a developer at
Obsidian Entertainment
, well known for his leadership role in the creation of
Fallout
.

BACKER_CHA_Kae_Polzech
GUID
ee1c3948-f0f1-4bab-88bf-ef1f89b9f2e6
Kae Polzech
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
You find a woman of early middle years dressed fine - if dirty - armor adorned with bright purple piping. A pair of long scars bisect her brow and jaw.
Though she stands at ease, a nervous energy thrums through her.
Kae was born in Aedyr, but spent most of her life traveling. She did most of her travel through
the Living Lands
, but recently took up to crossing the Deadfire. She is employed at a university as a tenured professor, and her travels keep her in the field, working on unlocking the secrets of Eora. Most of her work focuses on the glorious madness of the Living Lands, which is also where she lost several research expeditions. Ahem. It gave rise to rumors that Kae is cursed, but really, it's just the risk that comes with the territory.
Interactions
This character has
other interactions
.
Kae offers training for
3,000
, giving +1 to Stealth and Metaphysics.
Behind the scenes
Kae Polzech is one of the few
backer created characters
.
Kae mentions that one of her colleagues, Ines, "got herself lost looking for what was essentially a big, prickly weed." This is likely a direct reference to
Dragon Age: Origins
, where the main character can be tasked with helping a mage named
Ines
find a Northern Prickleweed in the
Awakening
DLC.

Kahn Hadret
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
A young woman lingers near the stage with a mug of ale clutched tight in her hands. Though she shows no interest in the dancers, the bags beneath her eyes speak to many long nights spent drinking in the tavern.
She looks lazily about the room until her gaze alights on you with interest.
Kahn is currently looking for
Oswald
, an elf who borrowed five thousand coppers from her and refused to pay it back. Understandably, she's annoyed about it. If he wasn't an old family friend - for four generations no less, due to him being an elf - and hadn't convinced her he was on the verge of creating a device that could use luminous adra to extend one's lifespan, she'd never have given him the money.
Kahn's the descendant of Admet Hadret and a minor Dyrwoodan noble. She despises the connection, as whenever someone realizes it, she suddenly becomes a Lady and people start doting on her. Understandably, she can't stand it.
Interactions
This character
starts
quests
.
Lost Dues in Good Faith
Quests
Lost Dues in Good Faith
: She asks you for help finding
Oswald
.

is a character in

.
Background
A young woman steps up to the edge of the cliff and peers down wearing an amused grin. She fingers the curve of a long hunting bow.
Kipeha is a Mataru of the Wahaki tribe, tasked with protecting the village. Anyone who wants to get in needs to go through her first.

Ori o Koīki
for details.
You can ask her to examine the
Infested Koīki
fruit. She will warn you not to eat it, as the wood-strangling wasps have planted their larvae within the fruit. Doing so would be fatal.

======================================================================
PAGE: Kuaru Spirit
CATEGORIES: Beast of Winter characters
URL: https://pillarsofeternity.fandom.com/wiki/Kuaru_Spirit
======================================================================

Kuaru Spirit
Biography and appearance
Game
Beast of Winter
Race
Island aumaua
Gender
Female
Gameplay
Location
The Shattered Passage
Kuaru Spirit
is a character in
Beast of Winter
. She can be found on the north-western tip of the main island, in
The Shattered Passage
. To get to her, you need to cross the pool of water by killing the aumaua spirit (a Shambling Soul, which drops
Kaihōa
) encountered near the entrance to
The Drowned Kingdom
.
Background
The spirit is busy repairing a bridge, although no amount of hammering on her part has any impact on the progression of repair. What happened to it is unknown.
Interactions
This character has
other interactions
.
She blocks the way across the bridge, you can use
Betrayal
to get by.
Bridge interaction
She will not let anyone, except Mataru, cross the bridge, by order of her ranga.
The Watcher can use
Betrayal
to pose as her ranga, telling her that the enemies have landed on the beach. This will prompt her to open the way forward, fixing the bridge in an instant, and follow your lead to charge the enemy. After her labors are done, she wonders where she should go. You can either point her towards oblivion, or return her to the Wheel by having her come with you.
Being allowed to cross the bridge gives the Watcher access to the portal, which in turn gives access to the
Glamfellen Soul
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Kusi
CATEGORIES: Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire characters
URL: https://pillarsofeternity.fandom.com/wiki/Kusi
======================================================================

Kusi
Biography and appearance
Game
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
Race
Island
aumaua
Gender
Female
Gameplay
Kusi
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
The girl panting before you, draped in tattered Roparu robes, bears a few bruises and cuts but looks otherwise unharmed. Beads of sweat comingle with trickling blood on her forehead.
Finally relaxing, she lowers the sword she's been swinging, letting the edge rest in the dirt. The pommel bears the form of a dog's head.
Kusi has tried clearing
the Gullet
of a pack of skuldr that have been preying on people for weeks, using a sword left to her by her father, promising she'd use it one day to defend the Deadfire. What he neglected to mention was the fact that she'd also need training to use it effectively.
Interactions
This character has
other interactions
.
Kusi is encountered at random while travelling through
Neketaka
, fighting off a pack of
Skuldr
. She will offer you
Griffin's Blade
if you managed to save her or will drop it if she didn't survive.
Saving Kusi leads to some extra dialogue. To keep her alive, use several casts of
Withdraw
,
Scroll of Withdraw
, or another spell that makes her untargetable.
One of the script choices before the fight draws foes' attention away from her (requires
Athletics
6) and gives Moderate Positive: Neketaka. Passing this check causes a single tough skuldr to continue attacking her.
Notes
Kusi can be hard to see, so use the Tab key to find her friendly blue circle.

Larro Bardatto
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
. He can initially be found in
Queen's Berth
, and later on within
Bardatto Estate
depending on the outcome of
Salt in the Wound
.
Background
A young member of the Bardatto family obsessed with honor and the family's vengiatta against the Valeras, Larro allows feelings to get in the way of business: He'd rather duel
Orso Valera
than attend family business meetings, further destabilizing the situation between the two.
Larro is the son of the family matriarch
Ezzali Bardatto
and the brother of
Nera Bardatto
. According to Nera, Larro and his friends often carouse at the tavern, the southewestern bridge, and behind the district's waterfall.
Interactions

involved in
quests
.

: He is the target of the search.

NPC_SD_Survivor_Solo
GUID
c203f480-cc7b-40fc-98b0-428b6fc9e205
Lone Survivor
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
His boots are slicked with grime. His clothes are filthy and rumpled from several days' wear, and his neck and hands are smeared in places with mud.
A pack rests at his heels, empty enough to have flopped into itself. It likely carries no more than his dwindling supplies.
A lone aumaua searching the Old City for treasure, having scaled the cliffs down from the Gullet. Packing about two weeks work of supplies, he quickly realised his situation after being unable to climb back out, and with the only exits being swarmed with grubs.
Interactions
This character has
other interactions
.
You can help him out of the
Old City
through a rather detailed interaction, leading you through all three parts of the undercity (see below).
Helping the Lone Survivor
You can initially save him by fighting through the ruins in the southeastern corner of the Overlook, immediately below the lift walkway. He'll ask you for help to clear a way out, and says the best way out of the old city is via the rivers that run down the cliffs and towards the ocean.
Kill the grubs in the southwestern corner of the Overlook (they only appear upon approaching), then return to tell him that you've cleared the path. He'll warn you about the
Giant Cave Grub
, then will proceed to the ruins.
If you didn't kill the grubs, you can lie to him (
Shady
,
Cruel
). He will be killed and his body can be found near the southwestern exit of the overlook.
Next, in the
Old City Ruins
, he can be found in the passage to the southeast waiting for you to clear a path ahead.
This time you'll have to clear the grubs just ahead to the northwest (again they only spawn upon approaching). Careful, since he will die in one hit should the grubs path back towards the tunnel.
Alternatively, if you opened the door in the Chamber of Waves to the southwest during
The Cornett's Call
, you can tell him to head that way instead. If you haven't yet killed the grubs ahead, he'll ask if the the route is clear. Again, you can lie to him (
Shady
/
Cruel
) and he will be killed.
You can ask for his torch to help you search ahead - though he is quite reluctant to be left in the dark, either of the options will result in him handing it to you. This doesn't affect the interaction in any way.
You can ask him how his supplies are holding up, then ask for some food. He'll give you 3
Glazed Chops
from his sachel of provisions.
Assuming you led him to safety, the lone survivor thanks you and asks that you visit him in
Port Maje
. Later he can be found in
Port Maje Harbor
, fishing near your ship's berth. Interacting with him, he thanks you once again and gives you a
Sapphire
and a
Cloak of Greater Deflection
(though he cannot be talked to in regular conversation).
Gallery
After helping him

Lucia Rivan
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
Dead for over two hundred years, Lucia Rivan was a
Darcozzi
paladin who helmed the
Fonferrus
, one of the
Vailian
flagships.
Rivan returned from the dead after being killed by
Yseyr
. The Berathian tracked the Fonferrus, losing the ensuing fight at the Battle of Dusken Isle. Yseyr retreated to
Neketaka
and became undead to safeguard the powerful sword that Rivan wielded during her defeat - the
Engoliero do Espirs
.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests
.

: Seizing her ship is the only way the Príncipi can hope to reach Ukaizo before other powers.

Marihi
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
A talented armored and weaponsmith, Marihi plies her trade in the Overlook, catering to the wealthy and the powerful, who care little for function and much more for form. While it doesn't utilize her talents as a blacksmith to the fullest, all that engraving and decorating pays the bills well and she gets to work with exotic materials.

merchant
.

.

BACKER_NPC_Mark_van_der_Bij

830616c2-08d1-42eb-b23e-15477fe77e93
Mark van der Bij
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
You find a man of middle years inspecting a metal tool unlike any you've seen. He has several similarly strange items on his belt, all quite clean and orderly. They look like the tools one might use to pull a tooth or shoe a horse, but much more delicate.
He wears pristine, cream-colored robes. The man's robes shimmer with a faint trace of arcane energy. Glyphs stitched into the hems and sleeves seem to be the source of the effect. The muzzle of an arquebus is visible just over his shoulder. His eyes brighten when he notices you.
Mark is a researcher in the medical sciences - not animancy, not necromancy, but actual medicine - and believes magic to be a crutch obstructing actual scientific progress. This makes him unpopular among most folk. Mark believes that this unpopularity led someone to assassinate his patient in order to discredit his work.
As such, he escaped into the Deadfire to pursue his work in peace and settled at Neketaka.
Interactions
This character has
other interactions
.
This character offers training (+1
Alchemy
, +1
Religion
) for
3,000
.
Behind the scenes
Mark van der Bij is one of the 10
backer created NPCs
, created as part of
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
's crowdfunding campaign.

Marofeto Liano
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
You find a man dressed in worn, dirty leather armor. His long, scraggly beard is encrusted with salt, his curling hair has clearly not seen a comb in some time, and the toenails of his bare fear are cracked and torn.
The only thing of any value that he carries is an amulet.
Marofeto is a former Goldpact Knight who was ejected from the order after a botched job. Since then, he wandered the Deadfire, rededicating himself to self-discipline and abstention from worldly distractions. In his view, it is through suffering that the soul becomes strong.
Interactions
This character has
other interactions
.
This character offers
training
(+1
Intimidate
, +1
Insight
) for
3,000
.
You can also obtain his amulet with
Intimidate
6 or
Bluff
/
Diplomacy
6, giving you
Claim and Refusal
.
If you obtain his amulet through the Intimidate check, he will refuse to train you.
Behind the scenes
Marofeto Liano is one of the 10
backer created NPCs
, created as part of
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
's crowdfunding campaign.

Mokeha
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
The aumaua woman steps sideways, angling herself towards you, and meets your gaze with an intense stare.
Mokeha is a proud woman who is a Mataru of the tribe and one of its protectors... But with little knowledge of the world outside of the village. As such, this leads to a lot of confusion, as she assumes the world operates according to Huana philosophy, when it really doesn't. This has recently surfaced in the altercation with
Rinco
.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests
.
Burning Bridges
This character has
other interactions
.
She does not talk to you if you already stole
Rinco's Coin Purse
from her.
Quests
Burning Bridges
: She is the culprit of the assault - or so she says.
Dialogue
Introductory dialogue
If the Watcher is a
moon godlike
"I did not think Clario's outsider to be one of Ngati's favored."
Mokeha's voice is low and halting. Her rigid frown softens, and she folds her arms across her chest.
If the Watcher is an
island aumaua
or has the
Deadfire Archipelago
background
"Do you come with the traders, brother/sister? Or have the Kahanga chased you from Neketaka? You are not one of ours."
Her lip curls dismissively.
If the Watcher is another
godlike
"Outsiders of every sort. This is what the Vailians have brought us."
Her scarred brow wrinkles, and her frown deepens into a somber grimace.
Otherwise
"I do not know you."
Her voice is quiet, but each word is clipped and harsh.

b62f5f79-9aff-4652-8544-24c36ec5af18
Muhai
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
. She can be found in her
estate
in the
Serpent's Crown
district of
Neketaka
.
Background
A Mataru of the Kahanga tribe, Muhai has recently passed away in her home. A proud, stubborn woman, her spirit instead clinged to life, demanding that the proper rites be executed before she passes to the wheel.
Of course, the situation is a bit more complicated: Muhai broke with the wahua and for that was sentenced to banishment from collective memory. Her crime? As a member of the Auweki tribe, who were fierce enemies of the Wapua, she purposefully led the latter's hunting party when they sought her counsel as navigator. As all Huana who are part of the Queen's domain are considered a single tribe, the Kahanga, this was a violation of the most basic tenets of their culture and law, leading to Muhai's banishment.
Interactions
This character
starts
quests
.
Her Last Request
Quests
Her Last Request
: She asks that you cremate her body at
The Sacred Stair
, dedicating it to
Magran
in death.

Naxiva ix Kirent
is a character in
Beast of Winter
.
Background
A prominent inquisitor of Engwith, Naxiva has been trapped in the White Void for a thousand years, reliving the trials she participated in, as a result of the horrific realization that she participated in an endless circus of atrocities. All in the name of peace and a better world. The trauma split her into two parts: The
chained spirit
and
Inquisitor Naxiva
, each tied to the other in a never-ending parade of horrors.

Nedunga
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
An elderly Roparu who would be normally sentenced to starve, the catastrophe that swept through his village on Sayuka was a blessing in disguise, as he got the opportunity to try and learn weaving rugs from
Osauro
. In return, he helps her fix anything she requires. The arrangement is unusual for the Huana, but despite living packed so densely, they both relish the opportunity to bridge gaps - especially Nedunga.
Interactions
This character has no special interactions.

Nera Bardatto
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
. She can initially be found in
Queen's Berth
, and later on within
Bardatto Estate
.
Background
A woman in fine clothes clutches a ledger in both hands. She searches the faces of passers-by, settling on yours with an uncertain frown.
Nera is a dutiful member of the Bardatto family, which runs the bank that backs the financial operations of the
Vailian Trading Company
. Her mother is the family matriarch
Ezzali Bardatto
.
When you meet her, Nera is looking for her brother,
Larro Bardatto
, who is skipping company meetings. Due to his run-ins with Valera family, their rival in the VTC, Larro may be in a bit of danger.
Interactions

starts
quests

: Nera requests that you locate her lazy brother, due for a Company meeting.

======================================================================
PAGE: Neriscyrlas
CATEGORIES: Beast of Winter characters
URL: https://pillarsofeternity.fandom.com/wiki/Neriscyrlas
======================================================================

Neriscyrlas
Biography and appearance
Game
Beast of Winter
Race
Lich
dragon
Gender
Female
Gameplay
Location
Temple of Decline
Neriscyrlas
is a character in
Beast of Winter
.
Background
A dragon capable of wielding wizardry, Neriscyrlas' pursuit of immortality drove her into the jaws of death. She persisted within the White Void for centuries, the edges of her soul slowly tattered by Rymrgand's incessant pull. Despite her condition, she supped from the very entropic energies tearing at her and developed the ability to propel herself from the Beyond, manifesting in the Here in search of further essence to anchor her to the living world - and fuel her undying ambition.
Four hundred years ago, she was one of the fiercest predators in the Deadfire, set on bending it to its will. Unrivaled by any kith or dragon, Neriscyrlas turned her gaze on the gods and decided to challenge them, so that she may remain safe from their ambitions, unlike the ancient three dragons slaved to their will through the
Guardian of Ukaizo
. However, in order to achieve the power necessary to challenge them, she needed to further increase her immense power. The artifacts sacrificed to Rymrgand at his temple, thrown into the White Void by the Glamfellen, were the perfect choice in her mind.
In her rush to seize the power, she attacked the temple and its worshipers, unleashing the eldritch energies and magic she controlled to blast through the legions of rime constructs and blast apart the defenders. However, she underestimated the religious zeal of the defenders: When she neared the Vydmath,
Rynhaedr
, first among the guards, opened the portal to the White Void using herself as a conduit. The dragon was consumed by the portal, while the resulting wave of frost froze every living creature in the temple on the spot. Neriscyrlas did not give up, however, even as the energies of the Void lapped at her, tearing apart her body.
She chained her soul to an ancient Engwithan phylactery, making it impossible for Rymrgand to destroy her, even inside his realm. As the dragon's mortal shell decayed, her power only increased, to the point that she could literally will herself into existence, assuming corporeal form in Eora for brief periods of time, but always inevitably sucked back. She requires essence - a lot of essence - to escape it permanently, motivated by the knowledge of the gods' real nature. After all, her mother was older than the manufactured gods of Engwith when she hatched her - older still than the gods are in 2828 AI.
Neriscyrlas' circumstances are unique, and
Eora
may never see her like again.
Interactions
This character is
involved in
quests
.
An Honored Guest
Death's Depthless Dominion
Quests
An Honored Guest
: Neriscyrlas is encountered at the end of the quest, as the Messenger of Rymrgand.
Death's Depthless Dominion
: Neriscyrlas is pursued throughout the quest as a favor to Rymrgand.

Nungata
is a character in
Pillars of Eternity II: Deadfire
.
Background
A woman with skin like hardened sailcloth sits upright and stares off to the distance, her lips held in a tight and thoughtful pinch. 
She blinks and sits even straighter as you cross her view.
Nungata is an elderly lady who retired to Neketaka after a lifetime of adventuring, violence, and great achievement. However, her life as a bounty hunter that followed the hunting of equally slippery creatures in the jungle has led to a great many foes in her life. She retired, but even a retired Mataru works for the betterment of the tribe. As such, she processes
Huana
bounties
.
She's worked with
Tekēhu
in the past - and remembers him well, for the godlike plundered half of her earnings after they took down a crab thief (though Tekēhu insists it was only a third).
Interactions
This character
starts
quests
.
Bounty - Beina
Bounty - Flamewalker Vessali
Bounty - The Steel Preacher
Bounty - Uamoru the Pretender
This character has
other interactions
.
She has unique dialogue with
Tekēhu
.
If you've completed the bounties for
Abocco
, she will mention this, though rather patronizingly.
Quests
Nungata hands out bounties.
